function change_level_now(pos,lvid,gvid,angle)
  local p = net_packet()
  p:w_begin(13)
  p:w_u16(gvid)
  p:w_u32(lvid)
  p:w_vec3(pos)
  p:w_vec3(angle)
  level.send(p,true)
end
